The Anniversary of Bhagwan Sri Ramakrishna. Sir,

We have great pleasure in inviting you to join us in celebrating the – the Anniversary of Bhagwan Ramakrishna Paramhansa. For the celebration of this great occasion and for the maintenance of the Alambazar Math funds are absolutely necessary. Yours obediently,

The only way of getting our divine nature manifested is by helping others do the same.

If there is inequality in nature still there must be equal chance for all– or if greater for some and for some less – the weaker should be given more chance than the stronger.1

M—has a tendency to put that stuff down everybody's throat, but that will make our movement a little sect. You keep separate from such attempts. At the same time, if people worship him as God, no harm. Neither encourage nor discourage. The masses will always have the person the higher ones, the principle, we want both. These will spoil everything. ‘‘The first should be last and the last first.’’‡
